Time Series Line Plot

Shows amplitude variations over time for each signal.

Useful for detecting patterns, trends, and anomalies in speech data.

Histogram (Amplitude Distribution)

Displays the frequency of amplitude values.

Helps analyze how values are distributed and detect outliers.

Box Plot (Feature Distribution)

Represents statistical distribution across multiple features.

Highlights median, quartiles, and potential outliers.

Population vs Sample Distribution

Population (yellow)

Histogram shows the distribution of all data from a dataset (full population). Density gives an idea of ​​how data values ​​are spread across the dataset.

Sample (grey)

A histogram shows the distribution of a subset (random sample) taken from a population. It provides a small representation of the population, showing how the sample approximates the full population distribution.
